#### What this PR does / why we need it:
This is a part of a larger effort to improve error handling in Topology Aware Scheduling (TAS). Currently, in workloads scheduled by TAS, whenever a even single node running a pod from this workload fails, there is no mechanism to replace it but the whole workload has to be evicted (without TAS, a standard K8s scheduler would replace this node https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/workloads/pods/#pods-and-controllers). 

This PR has:
- A new node failure controller that upon node failure adds the name of the failed node to Annotation on each affected workload.

In the next step, we want to use this information to find a new topology assignment and replace the failed node. 

#### Which issue(s) this PR fixes:
<!--
*Automatically closes linked issue when PR is merged.
Usage: `Fixes #<issue number>`, or `Fixes (paste link of issue)`.
_If PR is about `failing-tests or flakes`, please post the related issues/tests in a comment and do not use `Fixes`_*
-->
Part of #5230

```diff
+

+		client: client,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName(NodeFailureControllerName),
+		clock:  clock.RealClock{},
+	}
+}
+

```

```diff
+const (
+	NodeFailureControllerName = "kueue-node-failure-controller"
+	NodeFailureDelay          = 30 * time.Second
+)
+
+// nodeFailureReconciler reconciles Nodes to detect failures and update affected Workloads
+type nodeFailureReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	clock  clock.Clock
+	log    logr.Logger
+}

+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=nodes,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=pods,verbs=get;list;watch

+
+func newNodeFailureReconciler(client client.Client) *nodeFailureReconciler {

+		client: client,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName(NodeFailureControllerName),
+		clock:  clock.RealClock{},
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager, cfg *config.Configuration) (string, error) {
+	return NodeFailureControllerName, builder.ControllerManagedBy(mgr).
+		Named(NodeFailureControllerName).
+		For(&corev1.Node{}, builder.WithPredicates(predicate.Funcs{
+			CreateFunc:  func(e event.CreateEvent) bool { return false },
+			UpdateFunc:  func(e event.UpdateEvent) bool { return true },
```

  WDYT about making this function a little more powerful, and returning true if and only if the readiness of node changed from `true` to `false`?

```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,201 @@
+/*

+Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+You may obtain a copy of the License at
+
+    http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
+

+distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package tas
+
+import (
+	"context"
+	"fmt"
+	"slices"
+	"time"
+
+	"github.com/go-logr/logr"
+	corev1 "k8s.io/api/core/v1"
+	apierrors "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/api/errors"
+	metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/types"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/sets"
+	"k8s.io/klog/v2"
+	"k8s.io/utils/clock"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/builder"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/event"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/predicate"
+
+	config "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/config/v1beta1"
+	kueuealpha "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1beta1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/controller/tas/indexer"
+	utilpod "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/util/pod"
+)
+
+const (
+	NodeFailureControllerName = "kueue-node-failure-controller"
+	NodeFailureDelay          = 30 * time.Second
+)
+
+// nodeFailureReconciler reconciles Nodes to detect failures and update affected Workloads
+type nodeFailureReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	clock  clock.Clock
+	log    logr.Logger
+}
+
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=nodes,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=pods,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads/status,verbs=get;patch;update
+
+func newNodeFailureReconciler(client client.Client) *nodeFailureReconciler {
+	return &nodeFailureReconciler{
+		client: client,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName(NodeFailureControllerName),
+		clock:  clock.RealClock{},
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager, cfg *config.Configuration) (string, error) {
+	return NodeFailureControllerName, builder.ControllerManagedBy(mgr).
+		Named(NodeFailureControllerName).
+		For(&corev1.Node{}, builder.WithPredicates(predicate.Funcs{
+			CreateFunc:  func(e event.CreateEvent) bool { return false },
+			UpdateFunc:  func(e event.UpdateEvent) bool { return true },
+			DeleteFunc:  func(e event.DeleteEvent) bool { return true },
+			GenericFunc: func(e event.GenericEvent) bool { return false },
+		})).
+		Complete(r)
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithValues("node", req.Name)
+	ctx = ctrl.LoggerInto(ctx, log)
+
+	log.V(3).Info("Getting node", "name", req.Name, "namespacename", req.NamespacedName)
+	var node corev1.Node
+	err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &node)
+	nodeExists := !apierrors.IsNotFound(err)
+	if err != nil && nodeExists {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to get Node")
+		return ctrl.Result{}, err
+	}
+
+	nodeIsReady := false
+	markFailed := false
+	var readyTransitionTime *metav1.Time
+	var readyStatus corev1.ConditionStatus
+	requeueAfter := time.Duration(0)
+	if nodeExists {
+		readyStatus, readyTransitionTime = r.getNodeConditionState(&node)
+		nodeIsReady = (readyStatus == corev1.ConditionTrue)
+		log.V(3).Info("Reconciling node", "found", nodeExists, "ready", nodeIsReady)
+		if readyTransitionTime != nil {
+			timeSinceNotReady := r.clock.Now().Sub(readyTransitionTime.Time)
+			if timeSinceNotReady >= NodeFailureDelay {
+				markFailed = true
+			} else {
+				requeueAfter = NodeFailureDelay - timeSinceNotReady
+			}
+		} else { // Node exists, not ready, but no transition time? Treat as failed immediately.
```

  Should we check the `nodeIsReady` value before assuming the node is not ready here?

```diff
+	corev1 "k8s.io/api/core/v1"
+	apierrors "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/api/errors"
+	metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/types"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/sets"
+	"k8s.io/klog/v2"
+	"k8s.io/utils/clock"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/builder"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/event"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/predicate"
+
+	config "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/config/v1beta1"
+	kueuealpha "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1beta1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/controller/tas/indexer"
+	utilpod "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/util/pod"
+)
+
+const (
+	NodeFailureControllerName = "kueue-node-failure-controller"
+	NodeFailureDelay          = 30 * time.Second
+)
+
+// nodeFailureReconciler reconciles Nodes to detect failures and update affected Workloads
+type nodeFailureReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	clock  clock.Clock
+	log    logr.Logger
+}
+
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=nodes,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=pods,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads/status,verbs=get;patch;update
+
+func newNodeFailureReconciler(client client.Client) *nodeFailureReconciler {
+	return &nodeFailureReconciler{
+		client: client,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName(NodeFailureControllerName),
+		clock:  clock.RealClock{},
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager, cfg *config.Configuration) (string, error) {
+	return NodeFailureControllerName, builder.ControllerManagedBy(mgr).
+		Named(NodeFailureControllerName).
+		For(&corev1.Node{}, builder.WithPredicates(predicate.Funcs{
+			CreateFunc:  func(e event.CreateEvent) bool { return false },
+			UpdateFunc:  func(e event.UpdateEvent) bool { return true },
+			DeleteFunc:  func(e event.DeleteEvent) bool { return true },
+			GenericFunc: func(e event.GenericEvent) bool { return false },
+		})).
+		Complete(r)
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithValues("node", req.Name)
+	ctx = ctrl.LoggerInto(ctx, log)
+
+	log.V(3).Info("Getting node", "name", req.Name, "namespacename", req.NamespacedName)
+	var node corev1.Node
+	err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &node)
+	nodeExists := !apierrors.IsNotFound(err)
+	if err != nil && nodeExists {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to get Node")
+		return ctrl.Result{}, err
+	}
+
+	nodeIsReady := false
+	markFailed := false
+	var readyTransitionTime *metav1.Time
+	var readyStatus corev1.ConditionStatus
+	requeueAfter := time.Duration(0)
+	if nodeExists {
+		readyStatus, readyTransitionTime = r.getNodeConditionState(&node)
+		nodeIsReady = (readyStatus == corev1.ConditionTrue)
+		log.V(3).Info("Reconciling node", "found", nodeExists, "ready", nodeIsReady)
+		if readyTransitionTime != nil {
+			timeSinceNotReady := r.clock.Now().Sub(readyTransitionTime.Time)
+			if timeSinceNotReady >= NodeFailureDelay {
+				markFailed = true
+			} else {
+				requeueAfter = NodeFailureDelay - timeSinceNotReady
+			}
+		} else { // Node exists, not ready, but no transition time? Treat as failed immediately.
```

```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,202 @@
```

```diff
+
+package tas
+
+import (
+	"context"
+	"fmt"
+	"slices"
+	"time"
+
+	"github.com/go-logr/logr"
+	corev1 "k8s.io/api/core/v1"
+	apierrors "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/api/errors"
+	metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/types"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/sets"
+	"k8s.io/klog/v2"
+	"k8s.io/utils/clock"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/builder"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/event"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/predicate"
+
+	config "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/config/v1beta1"
+	kueuealpha "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1beta1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/controller/tas/indexer"
+	utilpod "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/util/pod"
+)
+
+const (
+	NodeFailureControllerName = "kueue-node-failure-controller"
+	NodeFailureDelay          = 30 * time.Second
+)
+
+// nodeFailureReconciler reconciles Nodes to detect failures and update affected Workloads
+type nodeFailureReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	clock  clock.Clock
+	log    logr.Logger
+}
+
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=nodes,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=pods,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads/status,verbs=get;patch;update
+
+func newNodeFailureReconciler(client client.Client) *nodeFailureReconciler {
+	return &nodeFailureReconciler{
+		client: client,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName(NodeFailureControllerName),
+		clock:  clock.RealClock{},
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager, cfg *config.Configuration) (string, error) {
+	return NodeFailureControllerName, builder.ControllerManagedBy(mgr).
+		Named(NodeFailureControllerName).
+		For(&corev1.Node{}, builder.WithPredicates(predicate.Funcs{
+			CreateFunc:  func(e event.CreateEvent) bool { return false },
+			UpdateFunc:  func(e event.UpdateEvent) bool { return true },
+			DeleteFunc:  func(e event.DeleteEvent) bool { return true },
+			GenericFunc: func(e event.GenericEvent) bool { return false },
+		})).
+		Complete(r)
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithValues("node", req.Name)
+	ctx = ctrl.LoggerInto(ctx, log)
+
+	log.V(3).Info("Getting node", "name", req.Name, "namespacename", req.NamespacedName)
+	var node corev1.Node
+	err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &node)
+	nodeExists := !apierrors.IsNotFound(err)
+	if err != nil && nodeExists {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to get Node")
+		return ctrl.Result{}, err
+	}
+
+	nodeIsReady := false
+	markFailed := false
+	var readyTransitionTime *metav1.Time
+	var readyStatus corev1.ConditionStatus
+	requeueAfter := time.Duration(0)
+	if nodeExists {
+		readyStatus, readyTransitionTime = r.getNodeConditionState(&node)
+		nodeIsReady = (readyStatus == corev1.ConditionTrue)
+		log.V(3).Info("Reconciling node", "found", nodeExists, "ready", nodeIsReady)
+		if nodeIsReady {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+		}
+		if readyTransitionTime != nil {
+			timeSinceNotReady := r.clock.Now().Sub(readyTransitionTime.Time)
+			if timeSinceNotReady >= NodeFailureDelay {
+				markFailed = true
+			} else {
+				requeueAfter = NodeFailureDelay - timeSinceNotReady
+			}
+		} else { // Node exists, not ready, but no transition time? Treat as failed immediately.
+			markFailed = true
+		}
+
+	} else {
+		log.V(3).Info("Node not found, assuming deleted")
+		markFailed = true
+	}
+
+	if markFailed {
+		updateErr := r.updateWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx, req.Name)
+		if updateErr != nil {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, updateErr
+		}
+		return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+	}
+	return ctrl.Result{RequeueAfter: requeueAfter}, nil
+}
+
+// updateWorkloadsForNode finds workloads with pods on the specified node
+// and updates their status based on whether the node is currently considered failed.
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) updateWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx context.Context, nodeName string) error {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	var podList corev1.PodList
+	if err := r.client.List(ctx, &podList, client.MatchingFields{indexer.PodNodeNameIndexKey: nodeName}); err != nil {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to list pods on node", "nodeName", nodeName)
+		return err
+	}
+	consideredWorkloads := sets.New[types.NamespacedName]()
+	var workloadPatchErrors []error
+
+	for i := range podList.Items {
+		pod := &podList.Items[i]
+		if _, found := pod.GetLabels()[kueuealpha.TASLabel]; !found {
+			// skip non TAS pods
+			continue
+		}
+		if utilpod.IsTerminated(pod) {
+			continue
+		}
+		wlName, found := pod.Annotations[kueuealpha.WorkloadAnnotation]
+		if !found {
+			continue
+		}
+		wlKey := types.NamespacedName{Name: wlName, Namespace: pod.Namespace}
+		if consideredWorkloads.Has(wlKey) {
+			continue
+		}
+		consideredWorkloads.Insert(wlKey)
+
+		var wl kueue.Workload
+		if err := r.client.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wl); err != nil {
+			if apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
+				log.V(4).Info("Workload not found for pod, skipping", "workload", wlKey, "pod", klog.KObj(pod))
+			} else {
+				log.Error(err, "Failed to get workload for pod", "workload", wlKey, "pod", klog.KObj(pod))
+				workloadPatchErrors = append(workloadPatchErrors, err)
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if !slices.Contains(wl.Status.NodesToReplace, nodeName) {
+			wl.Status.NodesToReplace = append(wl.Status.NodesToReplace, nodeName)
+			log.V(4).Info("Adding node to workload failed list", "workload", wlKey, "nodeName", nodeName)
+			if err := r.client.Status().Update(ctx, &wl); err != nil {
+				log.Error(err, "Failed to update workload status", "workload", wlKey)
+				workloadPatchErrors = append(workloadPatchErrors, err)
+			} else {
+				log.V(3).Info("Successfully updated workload status", "workload", wlKey, "failedNodes", wl.Status.NodesToReplace)
+			}
+		}
+	}
+	if len(workloadPatchErrors) > 0 {
+		return fmt.Errorf("encountered %d errors updating workloads for node %s: %w", len(workloadPatchErrors), nodeName, workloadPatchErrors[0])
```

  Can we use logger for that?

### Review by [@PBundyra](https://github.com/PBundyra) (commented) — 2025-05-07T15:54:36Z

```diff
+
+package tas
+
+import (
+	"context"
+	"fmt"
+	"slices"
+	"time"
+
+	"github.com/go-logr/logr"
+	corev1 "k8s.io/api/core/v1"
+	apierrors "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/api/errors"
+	metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/types"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/sets"
+	"k8s.io/klog/v2"
+	"k8s.io/utils/clock"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/builder"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/event"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/predicate"
+
+	config "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/config/v1beta1"
+	kueuealpha "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1beta1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/controller/tas/indexer"
+	utilpod "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/util/pod"
+)
+
+const (
+	NodeFailureControllerName = "kueue-node-failure-controller"
+	NodeFailureDelay          = 30 * time.Second
+)
+
+// nodeFailureReconciler reconciles Nodes to detect failures and update affected Workloads
+type nodeFailureReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	clock  clock.Clock
+	log    logr.Logger
+}
+
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=nodes,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=pods,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads/status,verbs=get;patch;update
+
+func newNodeFailureReconciler(client client.Client) *nodeFailureReconciler {
+	return &nodeFailureReconciler{
+		client: client,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName(NodeFailureControllerName),
+		clock:  clock.RealClock{},
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager, cfg *config.Configuration) (string, error) {
+	return NodeFailureControllerName, builder.ControllerManagedBy(mgr).
+		Named(NodeFailureControllerName).
+		For(&corev1.Node{}, builder.WithPredicates(predicate.Funcs{
+			CreateFunc:  func(e event.CreateEvent) bool { return false },
+			UpdateFunc:  func(e event.UpdateEvent) bool { return true },
+			DeleteFunc:  func(e event.DeleteEvent) bool { return true },
+			GenericFunc: func(e event.GenericEvent) bool { return false },
+		})).
+		Complete(r)
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithValues("node", req.Name)
+	ctx = ctrl.LoggerInto(ctx, log)
+
+	log.V(3).Info("Getting node", "name", req.Name, "namespacename", req.NamespacedName)
+	var node corev1.Node
+	err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &node)
+	nodeExists := !apierrors.IsNotFound(err)
+	if err != nil && nodeExists {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to get Node")
+		return ctrl.Result{}, err
+	}
+
+	nodeIsReady := false
+	markFailed := false
+	var readyTransitionTime *metav1.Time
+	var readyStatus corev1.ConditionStatus
+	requeueAfter := time.Duration(0)
+	if nodeExists {
+		readyStatus, readyTransitionTime = r.getNodeConditionState(&node)
+		nodeIsReady = (readyStatus == corev1.ConditionTrue)
+		log.V(3).Info("Reconciling node", "found", nodeExists, "ready", nodeIsReady)
+		if nodeIsReady {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+		}
+		if readyTransitionTime != nil {
+			timeSinceNotReady := r.clock.Now().Sub(readyTransitionTime.Time)
+			if timeSinceNotReady >= NodeFailureDelay {
+				markFailed = true
+			} else {
+				requeueAfter = NodeFailureDelay - timeSinceNotReady
+			}
+		} else { // Node exists, not ready, but no transition time? Treat as failed immediately.
+			markFailed = true
+		}
+
+	} else {
+		log.V(3).Info("Node not found, assuming deleted")
+		markFailed = true
+	}
+
+	if markFailed {
+		updateErr := r.updateWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx, req.Name)
+		if updateErr != nil {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, updateErr
+		}
+		return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+	}
+	return ctrl.Result{RequeueAfter: requeueAfter}, nil
+}
+
+// updateWorkloadsForNode finds workloads with pods on the specified node
+// and updates their status based on whether the node is currently considered failed.
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) updateWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx context.Context, nodeName string) error {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	var podList corev1.PodList
+	if err := r.client.List(ctx, &podList, client.MatchingFields{indexer.PodNodeNameIndexKey: nodeName}); err != nil {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to list pods on node", "nodeName", nodeName)
+		return err
+	}
+	consideredWorkloads := sets.New[types.NamespacedName]()
+	var workloadPatchErrors []error
+
+	for i := range podList.Items {
+		pod := &podList.Items[i]
+		if _, found := pod.GetLabels()[kueuealpha.TASLabel]; !found {
+			// skip non TAS pods
+			continue
+		}
+		if utilpod.IsTerminated(pod) {
+			continue
+		}
+		wlName, found := pod.Annotations[kueuealpha.WorkloadAnnotation]
+		if !found {
+			continue
+		}
+		wlKey := types.NamespacedName{Name: wlName, Namespace: pod.Namespace}
+		if consideredWorkloads.Has(wlKey) {
+			continue
+		}
+		consideredWorkloads.Insert(wlKey)
+
+		var wl kueue.Workload
+		if err := r.client.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wl); err != nil {
+			if apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
+				log.V(4).Info("Workload not found for pod, skipping", "workload", wlKey, "pod", klog.KObj(pod))
+			} else {
+				log.Error(err, "Failed to get workload for pod", "workload", wlKey, "pod", klog.KObj(pod))
+				workloadPatchErrors = append(workloadPatchErrors, err)
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if !slices.Contains(wl.Status.NodesToReplace, nodeName) {
+			wl.Status.NodesToReplace = append(wl.Status.NodesToReplace, nodeName)
+			log.V(4).Info("Adding node to workload failed list", "workload", wlKey, "nodeName", nodeName)
+			if err := r.client.Status().Update(ctx, &wl); err != nil {
+				log.Error(err, "Failed to update workload status", "workload", wlKey)
+				workloadPatchErrors = append(workloadPatchErrors, err)
+			} else {
+				log.V(3).Info("Successfully updated workload status", "workload", wlKey, "failedNodes", wl.Status.NodesToReplace)
+			}
+		}
```

  WDYT about moving it to a separate loop that loops over `consideredWorkloads`

```diff
+			DeleteFunc:  func(e event.DeleteEvent) bool { return true },

+		})).
+		Complete(r)
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithValues("node", req.Name)
+	ctx = ctrl.LoggerInto(ctx, log)
+

+	var node corev1.Node
+	err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &node)
+	nodeExists := !apierrors.IsNotFound(err)
+	if err != nil && nodeExists {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to get Node")
+		return ctrl.Result{}, err
+	}
+
+	nodeIsReady := false
+	markFailed := false
+	var readyTransitionTime *metav1.Time
+	var readyStatus corev1.ConditionStatus
+	requeueAfter := time.Duration(0)
+	if nodeExists {

+		nodeIsReady = (readyStatus == corev1.ConditionTrue)
+		log.V(3).Info("Reconciling node", "found", nodeExists, "ready", nodeIsReady)
+		if nodeIsReady {
```

```diff
+		if readyTransitionTime != nil {
+			timeSinceNotReady := r.clock.Now().Sub(readyTransitionTime.Time)
+			if timeSinceNotReady >= NodeFailureDelay {
+				markFailed = true
+			} else {
+				requeueAfter = NodeFailureDelay - timeSinceNotReady
+			}
+		} else { // Node exists, not ready, but no transition time? Treat as failed immediately.
+			markFailed = true
+		}
+
+	} else {
+		log.V(3).Info("Node not found, assuming deleted")
+		markFailed = true
+	}
+
+	if markFailed {
+		updateErr := r.updateWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx, req.Name)
+		if updateErr != nil {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, updateErr
+		}
+		return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+	}
+	return ctrl.Result{RequeueAfter: requeueAfter}, nil
+}
+
+// updateWorkloadsForNode finds workloads with pods on the specified node
+// and updates their status based on whether the node is currently considered failed.
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) updateWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx context.Context, nodeName string) error {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	var podList corev1.PodList
+	if err := r.client.List(ctx, &podList, client.MatchingFields{indexer.PodNodeNameIndexKey: nodeName}); err != nil {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to list pods on node", "nodeName", nodeName)
+		return err
+	}
+	consideredWorkloads := sets.New[types.NamespacedName]()
+	var workloadPatchErrors []error
+
+	for i := range podList.Items {
+		pod := &podList.Items[i]
```

  ```suggestion
  	for _, pod  := range podList.Items {
  ```
  Nit, wdyt about such a refactoring for it to be a little more conventional

- **pkg/controller/tas/node_failure_controller.go:188** by [@pajakd](https://github.com/pajakd) — 2025-05-08T09:20:57Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,202 @@
+/*
+Copyright The Kubernetes Authors.
+

+you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.

+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package tas
+
+import (
+	"context"
+	"fmt"
+	"slices"
+	"time"
+
+	"github.com/go-logr/logr"
+	corev1 "k8s.io/api/core/v1"
+	apierrors "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/api/errors"
+	metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/types"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/sets"
+	"k8s.io/klog/v2"
+	"k8s.io/utils/clock"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/builder"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/event"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/predicate"
+
+	config "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/config/v1beta1"
+	kueuealpha "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1beta1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/controller/tas/indexer"
+	utilpod "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/util/pod"
+)
+
+const (
+	NodeFailureControllerName = "kueue-node-failure-controller"
+	NodeFailureDelay          = 30 * time.Second
+)
+
+// nodeFailureReconciler reconciles Nodes to detect failures and update affected Workloads
+type nodeFailureReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	clock  clock.Clock
+	log    logr.Logger
+}
+
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=nodes,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=pods,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads/status,verbs=get;patch;update
+
+func newNodeFailureReconciler(client client.Client) *nodeFailureReconciler {
+	return &nodeFailureReconciler{
+		client: client,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName(NodeFailureControllerName),
+		clock:  clock.RealClock{},
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager, cfg *config.Configuration) (string, error) {
+	return NodeFailureControllerName, builder.ControllerManagedBy(mgr).
+		Named(NodeFailureControllerName).
+		For(&corev1.Node{}, builder.WithPredicates(predicate.Funcs{
+			CreateFunc:  func(e event.CreateEvent) bool { return false },
+			UpdateFunc:  func(e event.UpdateEvent) bool { return true },
+			DeleteFunc:  func(e event.DeleteEvent) bool { return true },
+			GenericFunc: func(e event.GenericEvent) bool { return false },
+		})).
+		Complete(r)
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithValues("node", req.Name)
+	ctx = ctrl.LoggerInto(ctx, log)
+
+	log.V(3).Info("Getting node", "name", req.Name, "namespacename", req.NamespacedName)
+	var node corev1.Node
+	err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &node)
+	nodeExists := !apierrors.IsNotFound(err)
+	if err != nil && nodeExists {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to get Node")
+		return ctrl.Result{}, err
+	}
+
+	nodeIsReady := false
+	markFailed := false
+	var readyTransitionTime *metav1.Time
+	var readyStatus corev1.ConditionStatus
+	requeueAfter := time.Duration(0)
+	if nodeExists {
+		readyStatus, readyTransitionTime = r.getNodeConditionState(&node)
+		nodeIsReady = (readyStatus == corev1.ConditionTrue)
+		log.V(3).Info("Reconciling node", "found", nodeExists, "ready", nodeIsReady)
+		if nodeIsReady {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+		}
+		if readyTransitionTime != nil {
+			timeSinceNotReady := r.clock.Now().Sub(readyTransitionTime.Time)
+			if timeSinceNotReady >= NodeFailureDelay {
+				markFailed = true
+			} else {
+				requeueAfter = NodeFailureDelay - timeSinceNotReady
+			}
+		} else { // Node exists, not ready, but no transition time? Treat as failed immediately.
+			markFailed = true
+		}
+
+	} else {
+		log.V(3).Info("Node not found, assuming deleted")
+		markFailed = true
+	}
+
+	if markFailed {
+		updateErr := r.updateWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx, req.Name)
+		if updateErr != nil {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, updateErr
+		}
+		return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+	}
+	return ctrl.Result{RequeueAfter: requeueAfter}, nil
+}
+
+// updateWorkloadsForNode finds workloads with pods on the specified node
+// and updates their status based on whether the node is currently considered failed.
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) updateWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx context.Context, nodeName string) error {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	var podList corev1.PodList
+	if err := r.client.List(ctx, &podList, client.MatchingFields{indexer.PodNodeNameIndexKey: nodeName}); err != nil {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to list pods on node", "nodeName", nodeName)
+		return err
+	}
+	consideredWorkloads := sets.New[types.NamespacedName]()
+	var workloadPatchErrors []error
+
+	for i := range podList.Items {
+		pod := &podList.Items[i]
+		if _, found := pod.GetLabels()[kueuealpha.TASLabel]; !found {
+			// skip non TAS pods
+			continue
+		}
+		if utilpod.IsTerminated(pod) {
+			continue
+		}
+		wlName, found := pod.Annotations[kueuealpha.WorkloadAnnotation]
+		if !found {
+			continue
+		}
+		wlKey := types.NamespacedName{Name: wlName, Namespace: pod.Namespace}
+		if consideredWorkloads.Has(wlKey) {
+			continue
+		}
+		consideredWorkloads.Insert(wlKey)
+
+		var wl kueue.Workload
+		if err := r.client.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wl); err != nil {
+			if apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
+				log.V(4).Info("Workload not found for pod, skipping", "workload", wlKey, "pod", klog.KObj(pod))
+			} else {
+				log.Error(err, "Failed to get workload for pod", "workload", wlKey, "pod", klog.KObj(pod))
+				workloadPatchErrors = append(workloadPatchErrors, err)
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if !slices.Contains(wl.Status.NodesToReplace, nodeName) {
+			wl.Status.NodesToReplace = append(wl.Status.NodesToReplace, nodeName)
+			log.V(4).Info("Adding node to workload failed list", "workload", wlKey, "nodeName", nodeName)
+			if err := r.client.Status().Update(ctx, &wl); err != nil {
+				log.Error(err, "Failed to update workload status", "workload", wlKey)
+				workloadPatchErrors = append(workloadPatchErrors, err)
+			} else {
+				log.V(3).Info("Successfully updated workload status", "workload", wlKey, "failedNodes", wl.Status.NodesToReplace)
+			}
+		}
+	}
+	if len(workloadPatchErrors) > 0 {
+		return fmt.Errorf("encountered %d errors updating workloads for node %s: %w", len(workloadPatchErrors), nodeName, workloadPatchErrors[0])
```

  We are doing multiple updates and each might fail. Even if the first update fails, we still try to update the other workloads (I think this is correct). But this means we might end up with multiple errors. We are logging each individual error (above) but we have to return a single one from this function. I agree that this looks strange so updated to errors.Join.

```diff
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to get Node")
+		return ctrl.Result{}, err
+	}
+
+	nodeIsReady := false
+	markFailed := false
+	var readyTransitionTime *metav1.Time
+	var readyStatus corev1.ConditionStatus
+	requeueAfter := time.Duration(0)
+	if nodeExists {
+		readyStatus, readyTransitionTime = r.getNodeConditionState(&node)
+		nodeIsReady = (readyStatus == corev1.ConditionTrue)
+		log.V(3).Info("Reconciling node", "found", nodeExists, "ready", nodeIsReady)
+		if nodeIsReady {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+		}
+		if readyTransitionTime != nil {
+			timeSinceNotReady := r.clock.Now().Sub(readyTransitionTime.Time)
+			if timeSinceNotReady >= NodeFailureDelay {
+				markFailed = true
+			} else {
+				requeueAfter = NodeFailureDelay - timeSinceNotReady
+			}
+		} else { // Node exists, not ready, but no transition time? Treat as failed immediately.
+			markFailed = true
+		}
+
+	} else {
+		log.V(3).Info("Node not found, assuming deleted")
+		markFailed = true
+	}
+
+	if markFailed {
+		updateErr := r.updateWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx, req.Name)
+		if updateErr != nil {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, updateErr
+		}
+		return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+	}
+	return ctrl.Result{RequeueAfter: requeueAfter}, nil
+}
+
+// updateWorkloadsForNode finds workloads with pods on the specified node
+// and updates their status based on whether the node is currently considered failed.
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) updateWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx context.Context, nodeName string) error {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	var podList corev1.PodList
+	if err := r.client.List(ctx, &podList, client.MatchingFields{indexer.PodNodeNameIndexKey: nodeName}); err != nil {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to list pods on node", "nodeName", nodeName)
+		return err
+	}
+	consideredWorkloads := sets.New[types.NamespacedName]()
+	var workloadPatchErrors []error
+
+	for i := range podList.Items {
+		pod := &podList.Items[i]
+		if _, found := pod.GetLabels()[kueuealpha.TASLabel]; !found {
+			// skip non TAS pods
+			continue
+		}
+		if utilpod.IsTerminated(pod) {
+			continue
+		}
+		wlName, found := pod.Annotations[kueuealpha.WorkloadAnnotation]
+		if !found {
+			continue
+		}
+		wlKey := types.NamespacedName{Name: wlName, Namespace: pod.Namespace}
+		if consideredWorkloads.Has(wlKey) {
+			continue
+		}
+		consideredWorkloads.Insert(wlKey)
+
+		var wl kueue.Workload
+		if err := r.client.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wl); err != nil {
+			if apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
+				log.V(4).Info("Workload not found for pod, skipping", "workload", wlKey, "pod", klog.KObj(pod))
+			} else {
+				log.Error(err, "Failed to get workload for pod", "workload", wlKey, "pod", klog.KObj(pod))
+				workloadPatchErrors = append(workloadPatchErrors, err)
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if !slices.Contains(wl.Status.NodesToReplace, nodeName) {
+			wl.Status.NodesToReplace = append(wl.Status.NodesToReplace, nodeName)
+			log.V(4).Info("Adding node to workload failed list", "workload", wlKey, "nodeName", nodeName)
+			if err := r.client.Status().Update(ctx, &wl); err != nil {
+				log.Error(err, "Failed to update workload status", "workload", wlKey)
+				workloadPatchErrors = append(workloadPatchErrors, err)
+			} else {
+				log.V(3).Info("Successfully updated workload status", "workload", wlKey, "failedNodes", wl.Status.NodesToReplace)
+			}
+		}
+	}
+	if len(workloadPatchErrors) > 0 {
+		return fmt.Errorf("encountered %d errors updating workloads for node %s: %w", len(workloadPatchErrors), nodeName, workloadPatchErrors[0])
```

  Oh I see, I misunderstood intention of this line

```diff
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/event"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/predicate"
+
+	config "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/config/v1beta1"
+	kueuealpha "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1beta1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/controller/tas/indexer"
+	utilpod "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/util/pod"
+)
+
+const (
+	NodeFailureControllerName = "kueue-node-failure-controller"
+	NodeFailureDelay          = 30 * time.Second
+)
+
+// nodeFailureReconciler reconciles Nodes to detect failures and update affected Workloads
+type nodeFailureReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	clock  clock.Clock
+	log    logr.Logger
+}
+
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=nodes,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=pods,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads/status,verbs=get;patch;update
+
+func newNodeFailureReconciler(client client.Client) *nodeFailureReconciler {
+	return &nodeFailureReconciler{
+		client: client,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName(NodeFailureControllerName),
+		clock:  clock.RealClock{},
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager, cfg *config.Configuration) (string, error) {
+	return NodeFailureControllerName, builder.ControllerManagedBy(mgr).
+		Named(NodeFailureControllerName).
+		For(&corev1.Node{}, builder.WithPredicates(predicate.Funcs{
+			CreateFunc:  func(e event.CreateEvent) bool { return false },
+			UpdateFunc:  func(e event.UpdateEvent) bool { return true },
+			DeleteFunc:  func(e event.DeleteEvent) bool { return true },
+			GenericFunc: func(e event.GenericEvent) bool { return false },
+		})).
+		Complete(r)
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithValues("node", req.Name)
+	ctx = ctrl.LoggerInto(ctx, log)
+
+	log.V(3).Info("Getting node", "name", req.Name, "namespacename", req.NamespacedName)
+	var node corev1.Node
+	err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &node)
+	nodeExists := !apierrors.IsNotFound(err)
+	if err != nil && nodeExists {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to get Node")
+		return ctrl.Result{}, err
+	}
+
+	nodeIsReady := false
+	markFailed := false
+	var readyTransitionTime *metav1.Time
+	var readyStatus corev1.ConditionStatus
+	requeueAfter := time.Duration(0)
+	if nodeExists {
+		readyStatus, readyTransitionTime = r.getNodeConditionState(&node)
```

  Sounds perfectly reasonable, how about using https://pkg.go.dev/k8s.io/kubernetes/pkg/controller/util/node#GetNodeCondition

  I wondering if we should return true here as well, in case of Kueue's restart. Let's say there is a Node with Ready=false condition, and Kueue for some reason goes down. After restart the controller receives Create event with already failed Node, instead of Update

```diff
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package tas
+
+import (
+	"context"
+	"fmt"
+	"slices"
+	"time"
+
+	"github.com/go-logr/logr"
+	corev1 "k8s.io/api/core/v1"
+	apierrors "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/api/errors"
+	metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/types"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/sets"
+	"k8s.io/klog/v2"
+	"k8s.io/utils/clock"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/builder"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/event"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/predicate"
+
+	config "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/config/v1beta1"
+	kueuealpha "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1beta1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/controller/tas/indexer"
+	utilpod "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/util/pod"
+)
+
+const (
+	NodeFailureControllerName = "kueue-node-failure-controller"
+	NodeFailureDelay          = 30 * time.Second
+)
+
+// nodeFailureReconciler reconciles Nodes to detect failures and update affected Workloads
+type nodeFailureReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	clock  clock.Clock
+	log    logr.Logger
+}
+
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=nodes,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=pods,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads/status,verbs=get;patch;update
+
+func newNodeFailureReconciler(client client.Client) *nodeFailureReconciler {
+	return &nodeFailureReconciler{
+		client: client,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName(NodeFailureControllerName),
+		clock:  clock.RealClock{},
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager, cfg *config.Configuration) (string, error) {
+	return NodeFailureControllerName, builder.ControllerManagedBy(mgr).
+		Named(NodeFailureControllerName).
+		For(&corev1.Node{}, builder.WithPredicates(predicate.Funcs{
+			CreateFunc:  func(e event.CreateEvent) bool { return false },
+			UpdateFunc:  func(e event.UpdateEvent) bool { return true },
+			DeleteFunc:  func(e event.DeleteEvent) bool { return true },
+			GenericFunc: func(e event.GenericEvent) bool { return false },
+		})).
+		Complete(r)
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithValues("node", req.Name)
+	ctx = ctrl.LoggerInto(ctx, log)
+
+	log.V(3).Info("Getting node", "name", req.Name, "namespacename", req.NamespacedName)
+	var node corev1.Node
+	err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &node)
+	nodeExists := !apierrors.IsNotFound(err)
+	if err != nil && nodeExists {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to get Node")
+		return ctrl.Result{}, err
+	}
+
+	nodeIsReady := false
+	markFailed := false
+	var readyTransitionTime *metav1.Time
+	var readyStatus corev1.ConditionStatus
+	requeueAfter := time.Duration(0)
+	if nodeExists {
+		readyStatus, readyTransitionTime = r.getNodeConditionState(&node)
+		nodeIsReady = (readyStatus == corev1.ConditionTrue)
+		log.V(3).Info("Reconciling node", "found", nodeExists, "ready", nodeIsReady)
+		if nodeIsReady {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+		}
+		if readyTransitionTime != nil {
+			timeSinceNotReady := r.clock.Now().Sub(readyTransitionTime.Time)
+			if timeSinceNotReady >= NodeFailureDelay {
+				markFailed = true
+			} else {
+				requeueAfter = NodeFailureDelay - timeSinceNotReady
+			}
+		} else { // Node exists, not ready, but no transition time? Treat as failed immediately.
+			markFailed = true
+		}
+
+	} else {
+		log.V(3).Info("Node not found, assuming deleted")
+		markFailed = true
+	}
+
+	if markFailed {
+		updateErr := r.updateWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx, req.Name)
+		if updateErr != nil {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, updateErr
+		}
+		return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+	}
+	return ctrl.Result{RequeueAfter: requeueAfter}, nil
+}
+
+// updateWorkloadsForNode finds workloads with pods on the specified node
+// and updates their status based on whether the node is currently considered failed.
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) updateWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx context.Context, nodeName string) error {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	var podList corev1.PodList
+	if err := r.client.List(ctx, &podList, client.MatchingFields{indexer.PodNodeNameIndexKey: nodeName}); err != nil {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to list pods on node", "nodeName", nodeName)
+		return err
+	}
+	consideredWorkloads := sets.New[types.NamespacedName]()
+	var workloadPatchErrors []error
+
+	for i := range podList.Items {
+		pod := &podList.Items[i]
+		if _, found := pod.GetLabels()[kueuealpha.TASLabel]; !found {
+			// skip non TAS pods
+			continue
+		}
+		if utilpod.IsTerminated(pod) {
+			continue
+		}
+		wlName, found := pod.Annotations[kueuealpha.WorkloadAnnotation]
+		if !found {
+			continue
+		}
+		wlKey := types.NamespacedName{Name: wlName, Namespace: pod.Namespace}
+		if consideredWorkloads.Has(wlKey) {
+			continue
+		}
```

```diff
+	metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"

+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/sets"

+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/builder"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/event"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/predicate"
+
+	config "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/config/v1beta1"
+	kueuealpha "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1beta1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/controller/tas/indexer"
+	utilpod "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/util/pod"
+)
+
+const (
+	NodeFailureControllerName = "kueue-node-failure-controller"
+	NodeFailureDelay          = 30 * time.Second
+)
+
+// nodeFailureReconciler reconciles Nodes to detect failures and update affected Workloads
+type nodeFailureReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	clock  clock.Clock
+	log    logr.Logger
+}
+
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=nodes,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=pods,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads/status,verbs=get;patch;update
+
+func newNodeFailureReconciler(client client.Client) *nodeFailureReconciler {
+	return &nodeFailureReconciler{
+		client: client,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName(NodeFailureControllerName),
+		clock:  clock.RealClock{},
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager, cfg *config.Configuration) (string, error) {
+	return NodeFailureControllerName, builder.ControllerManagedBy(mgr).
+		Named(NodeFailureControllerName).
+		For(&corev1.Node{}, builder.WithPredicates(predicate.Funcs{
+			CreateFunc:  func(e event.CreateEvent) bool { return false },
+			UpdateFunc:  func(e event.UpdateEvent) bool { return true },
+			DeleteFunc:  func(e event.DeleteEvent) bool { return true },
+			GenericFunc: func(e event.GenericEvent) bool { return false },
+		})).
+		Complete(r)
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithValues("node", req.Name)
+	ctx = ctrl.LoggerInto(ctx, log)
+
+	log.V(3).Info("Getting node", "name", req.Name, "namespacename", req.NamespacedName)
+	var node corev1.Node
+	err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &node)
+	nodeExists := !apierrors.IsNotFound(err)
+	if err != nil && nodeExists {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to get Node")
+		return ctrl.Result{}, err
+	}
+
+	nodeIsReady := false
+	markFailed := false
+	var readyTransitionTime *metav1.Time
+	var readyStatus corev1.ConditionStatus
+	requeueAfter := time.Duration(0)
+	if nodeExists {
+		readyStatus, readyTransitionTime = r.getNodeConditionState(&node)
+		nodeIsReady = (readyStatus == corev1.ConditionTrue)
+		log.V(3).Info("Reconciling node", "found", nodeExists, "ready", nodeIsReady)
+		if nodeIsReady {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+		}
+		if readyTransitionTime != nil {
+			timeSinceNotReady := r.clock.Now().Sub(readyTransitionTime.Time)
+			if timeSinceNotReady >= NodeFailureDelay {
+				markFailed = true
+			} else {
+				requeueAfter = NodeFailureDelay - timeSinceNotReady
+			}
+		} else { // Node exists, not ready, but no transition time? Treat as failed immediately.
+			markFailed = true
+		}
+
+	} else {
+		log.V(3).Info("Node not found, assuming deleted")
+		markFailed = true
+	}
+
+	if markFailed {
+		updateErr := r.updateWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx, req.Name)
+		if updateErr != nil {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, updateErr
+		}
+		return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+	}
+	return ctrl.Result{RequeueAfter: requeueAfter}, nil
+}
+
+// updateWorkloadsForNode finds workloads with pods on the specified node
+// and updates their status based on whether the node is currently considered failed.
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) updateWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx context.Context, nodeName string) error {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	var podList corev1.PodList
+	if err := r.client.List(ctx, &podList, client.MatchingFields{indexer.PodNodeNameIndexKey: nodeName}); err != nil {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to list pods on node", "nodeName", nodeName)
+		return err
+	}
+	consideredWorkloads := sets.New[types.NamespacedName]()
+	var workloadPatchErrors []error
+
+	for i := range podList.Items {
+		pod := &podList.Items[i]
+		if _, found := pod.GetLabels()[kueuealpha.TASLabel]; !found {
+			// skip non TAS pods
+			continue
+		}
+		if utilpod.IsTerminated(pod) {
+			continue
+		}
+		wlName, found := pod.Annotations[kueuealpha.WorkloadAnnotation]
+		if !found {
+			continue
+		}
+		wlKey := types.NamespacedName{Name: wlName, Namespace: pod.Namespace}
+		if consideredWorkloads.Has(wlKey) {
+			continue
+		}
+		consideredWorkloads.Insert(wlKey)
+
+		var wl kueue.Workload
+		if err := r.client.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wl); err != nil {
+			if apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
+				log.V(4).Info("Workload not found for pod, skipping", "workload", wlKey, "pod", klog.KObj(pod))
+			} else {
+				log.Error(err, "Failed to get workload for pod", "workload", wlKey, "pod", klog.KObj(pod))
+				workloadPatchErrors = append(workloadPatchErrors, err)
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if !slices.Contains(wl.Status.NodesToReplace, nodeName) {
+			wl.Status.NodesToReplace = append(wl.Status.NodesToReplace, nodeName)
+			log.V(4).Info("Adding node to workload failed list", "workload", wlKey, "nodeName", nodeName)
+			if err := r.client.Status().Update(ctx, &wl); err != nil {
+				log.Error(err, "Failed to update workload status", "workload", wlKey)
+				workloadPatchErrors = append(workloadPatchErrors, err)
+			} else {
+				log.V(3).Info("Successfully updated workload status", "workload", wlKey, "failedNodes", wl.Status.NodesToReplace)
+			}
+		}
```

```diff
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/types"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/sets"
+	"k8s.io/klog/v2"
+	"k8s.io/utils/clock"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/builder"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/event"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/handler"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/predicate"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/reconcile"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/source"
+
+	config "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/config/v1beta1"
+	kueuealpha "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1beta1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/controller/tas/indexer"
+	utilpod "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/util/pod"
+	utiltas "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/util/tas"
+)
+
+const (
+	NodeFailureControllerName = "kueue-node-failure-controller"
+	// NodeToReplaceAnnotation is the annotation key on a Workload to store comma-separated list of failed node names.
+	NodeToReplaceAnnotation = "kueue.x-k8s.io/node-to-replace"
+	NodeFailureDelay        = 30 * time.Second
+)
+
+// nodeFailureReconciler reconciles Nodes to detect failures and update affected Workloads
+type nodeFailureReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	clock  clock.Clock
+	log    logr.Logger
+}
+
+var _ reconcile.Reconciler = (*nodeFailureReconciler)(nil)
+var _ predicate.TypedPredicate[*corev1.Node] = (*nodeFailureReconciler)(nil)
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Generic(event.TypedGenericEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	return false
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Create(e event.TypedCreateEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	return true
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Update(e event.TypedUpdateEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	newNode := e.ObjectNew
+	if newNode == nil {
+		r.log.V(4).Info("Update event with nil object")
+		return false
+	}
+	if !utiltas.IsNodeStatusConditionTrue(newNode.Status.Conditions, corev1.NodeReady) {
+		r.log.V(4).Info("NodeReady is not true", "node", klog.KObj(newNode))
+		return true
+	}
+	r.log.V(5).Info("Node update does not warrant reconcile for failure detection", "node", klog.KObj(newNode))
+	return false
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Delete(e event.TypedDeleteEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	return true
+}
+
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=nodes,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=pods,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads,verbs=get;list;watch;patch
+
+func newNodeFailureReconciler(client client.Client) *nodeFailureReconciler {
+	return &nodeFailureReconciler{
+		client: client,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName(NodeFailureControllerName),
+		clock:  clock.RealClock{},
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager, cfg *config.Configuration) (string, error) {
+	return NodeFailureControllerName, builder.ControllerManagedBy(mgr).
+		Named(NodeFailureControllerName).
+		WatchesRawSource(source.TypedKind(
+			mgr.GetCache(),
+			&corev1.Node{},
+			&handler.TypedEnqueueRequestForObject[*corev1.Node]{},
+			r,
+		)).
+		For(&corev1.Node{}).
```

```diff
+// nodeFailureReconciler reconciles Nodes to detect failures and update affected Workloads
+type nodeFailureReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	clock  clock.Clock
+	log    logr.Logger
+}
+
+var _ reconcile.Reconciler = (*nodeFailureReconciler)(nil)
+var _ predicate.TypedPredicate[*corev1.Node] = (*nodeFailureReconciler)(nil)

+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Generic(event.TypedGenericEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	return false
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Create(e event.TypedCreateEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	return true
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Update(e event.TypedUpdateEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	newNode := e.ObjectNew
+	if newNode == nil {
+		r.log.V(4).Info("Update event with nil object")
+		return false
+	}

+		r.log.V(4).Info("NodeReady is not true", "node", klog.KObj(newNode))
+		return true
+	}
+	r.log.V(5).Info("Node update does not warrant reconcile for failure detection", "node", klog.KObj(newNode))
+	return false

+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Delete(e event.TypedDeleteEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	return true
+}
```

```diff
+			DeleteFunc:  func(e event.DeleteEvent) bool { return true },
+			GenericFunc: func(e event.GenericEvent) bool { return false },
+		})).
+		Complete(r)
+}

+	var node corev1.Node
+	err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &node)
+	nodeExists := !apierrors.IsNotFound(err)
+	if err != nil && nodeExists {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to get Node")
```

- **pkg/controller/tas/node_failure_controller.go:216** by [@PBundyra](https://github.com/PBundyra) — 2025-05-09T09:49:41Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,230 @@
+/*
+Copyright The Kubernetes Authors.
+
+Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+You may obtain a copy of the License at
+
+    http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
+
+Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
+distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package tas
+
+import (
+	"context"
+	"errors"
+
+	"github.com/go-logr/logr"
+	corev1 "k8s.io/api/core/v1"
+	apierrors "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/api/errors"
+	metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/types"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/sets"
+	"k8s.io/klog/v2"
+	"k8s.io/utils/clock"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/builder"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/event"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/handler"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/predicate"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/reconcile"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/source"
+
+	config "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/config/v1beta1"
+	kueuealpha "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1beta1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/controller/tas/indexer"
+	utilpod "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/util/pod"
+	utiltas "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/util/tas"
+)
+
+// nodeFailureReconciler reconciles Nodes to detect failures and update affected Workloads
+type nodeFailureReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	clock  clock.Clock
+	log    logr.Logger
+}
+
+var _ reconcile.Reconciler = (*nodeFailureReconciler)(nil)
+var _ predicate.TypedPredicate[*corev1.Node] = (*nodeFailureReconciler)(nil)
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Generic(event.TypedGenericEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	return false
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Create(e event.TypedCreateEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	return true
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Update(e event.TypedUpdateEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	newNode := e.ObjectNew
+	if newNode == nil {
+		r.log.V(4).Info("Update event with nil object")
+		return false
+	}
+	if !utiltas.IsNodeStatusConditionTrue(newNode.Status.Conditions, corev1.NodeReady) {
+		r.log.V(4).Info("NodeReady is not true", "node", klog.KObj(newNode))
+		return true
+	}
+	r.log.V(5).Info("Node update does not warrant reconcile for failure detection", "node", klog.KObj(newNode))
+	return false
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Delete(e event.TypedDeleteEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	return true
+}
+
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=nodes,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=pods,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads,verbs=get;list;watch;patch
+
+func newNodeFailureReconciler(client client.Client) *nodeFailureReconciler {
+	return &nodeFailureReconciler{
+		client: client,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName(TASNodeFailureController),
+		clock:  clock.RealClock{},
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager, cfg *config.Configuration) (string, error) {
+	return TASNodeFailureController, builder.ControllerManagedBy(mgr).
+		Named(TASNodeFailureController).
+		WatchesRawSource(source.TypedKind(
+			mgr.GetCache(),
+			&corev1.Node{},
+			&handler.TypedEnqueueRequestForObject[*corev1.Node]{},
+			r,
+		)).
+		For(&corev1.Node{}).
+		Complete(r)
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithValues("node", req.Name)
+	ctx = ctrl.LoggerInto(ctx, log)
+
+	log.V(3).Info("Getting node", "name", req.Name, "namespacename", req.NamespacedName)
+	var node corev1.Node
+	err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &node)
+	nodeExists := !apierrors.IsNotFound(err)
+	if err != nil && nodeExists {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to get Node")
+		return ctrl.Result{}, err
+	}
+
+	markFailed := false
+	var readyTransitionTime *metav1.Time
+	var readyStatus corev1.ConditionStatus
+	if nodeExists {
+		readyStatus, readyTransitionTime = r.getNodeConditionState(&node)
+		if readyStatus == corev1.ConditionTrue {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+		}
+		if readyTransitionTime != nil {
+			timeSinceNotReady := r.clock.Now().Sub(readyTransitionTime.Time)
+			if timeSinceNotReady >= NodeFailureDelay {
+				markFailed = true
+			} else {
+				return ctrl.Result{RequeueAfter: NodeFailureDelay - timeSinceNotReady}, nil
+			}
+		} else { // Node exists, not ready, but no transition time? Treat as failed immediately.
+			markFailed = true
+			log.V(2).Info("Node is not ready and NodeReady condition is missing or has an unexpected status, marking as failed immediately", "nodeName", node.Name)
+		}
+	} else {
+		log.V(3).Info("Node not found, assuming deleted")
+		markFailed = true
+	}
+
+	if markFailed {
+		if patchErr := r.patchWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx, req.Name); patchErr != nil {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, patchErr
+		}
+	}
+	return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+}
+
+// patchWorkloadsForNode finds workloads with pods on the specified node
+// and patches their status based on whether the node is currently considered failed.
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) patchWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx context.Context, nodeName string) error {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	var podList corev1.PodList
+	if err := r.client.List(ctx, &podList, client.MatchingFields{indexer.PodNodeNameIndexKey: nodeName}); err != nil {
+		log.V(2).Error(err, "Failed to list pods on node", "nodeName", nodeName)
+		return err
+	}
+	workloadsToProcess := sets.New[types.NamespacedName]()
+	for _, pod := range podList.Items {
+		if _, found := pod.GetLabels()[kueuealpha.TASLabel]; !found {
+			// skip non TAS pods
+			continue
+		}
+		if utilpod.IsTerminated(&pod) {
+			continue
+		}
+		wlName, found := pod.Annotations[kueuealpha.WorkloadAnnotation]
+		if !found {
+			continue
+		}
+		workloadsToProcess.Insert(types.NamespacedName{Name: wlName, Namespace: pod.Namespace})
+	}
+	var workloadProcessingErrors []error
+	for _, wlKey := range workloadsToProcess.UnsortedList() {
+		var wl kueue.Workload
+		if err := r.client.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wl); err != nil {
+			if apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
+				log.V(4).Info("Workload not found, skipping", "workload", wlKey)
+			} else {
+				log.V(2).Error(err, "Failed to get workload", "workload", wlKey)
+				workloadProcessingErrors = append(workloadProcessingErrors, err)
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		originalWl := wl.DeepCopy()
+		currentAnnotations := wl.GetAnnotations()
+		if currentAnnotations == nil {
+			currentAnnotations = make(map[string]string)
+		}
+		existingFailedNode, ok := currentAnnotations[kueuealpha.NodeToReplaceAnnotation]
+		if ok && existingFailedNode != "" && existingFailedNode != nodeName {
+			// TODO in this case we will start eviction of the workload due to multiple failed nodes
+			return nil
+		}
+		if ok && existingFailedNode == nodeName {
+			// nothing to do
+			return nil
+		}
+		currentAnnotations[kueuealpha.NodeToReplaceAnnotation] = nodeName
+		wl.SetAnnotations(currentAnnotations)
+		log.V(4).Info("Adding failed node to workload annotation", "workload", wlKey, "nodeName", nodeName)
+		if err := r.client.Patch(ctx, &wl, client.MergeFrom(originalWl)); err != nil {
+			log.V(2).Error(err, "Failed to patch workload with annotation", "workload", wlKey)
+			workloadProcessingErrors = append(workloadProcessingErrors, err)
+		} else {
+			log.V(3).Info("Successfully patched workload with annotation", "workload", wlKey, "failedNodesAnnotation", currentAnnotations[kueuealpha.NodeToReplaceAnnotation])
+		}
+	}
+	if len(workloadProcessingErrors) > 0 {
+		return errors.Join(workloadProcessingErrors...)
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+// getNodeConditionState returns the status and last transition time of the NodeReady condition.
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) getNodeConditionState(node *corev1.Node) (status corev1.ConditionStatus, transitionTime *metav1.Time) {
```

  Can we make this function more generic so a caller can pass the type of the cond, or name it more explicitly it's for Ready cond?

```diff
+// nodeFailureReconciler reconciles Nodes to detect failures and update affected Workloads
+type nodeFailureReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	clock  clock.Clock
+	log    logr.Logger
+}
+
+var _ reconcile.Reconciler = (*nodeFailureReconciler)(nil)
+var _ predicate.TypedPredicate[*corev1.Node] = (*nodeFailureReconciler)(nil)
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Generic(event.TypedGenericEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	return false
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Create(e event.TypedCreateEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	return true
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Update(e event.TypedUpdateEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	newNode := e.ObjectNew
+	if newNode == nil {
+		r.log.V(4).Info("Update event with nil object")
+		return false
+	}
+	if !utiltas.IsNodeStatusConditionTrue(newNode.Status.Conditions, corev1.NodeReady) {
+		r.log.V(4).Info("NodeReady is not true", "node", klog.KObj(newNode))
+		return true
+	}
+	r.log.V(5).Info("Node update does not warrant reconcile for failure detection", "node", klog.KObj(newNode))
+	return false
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Delete(e event.TypedDeleteEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	return true
+}
+
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=nodes,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=pods,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads,verbs=get;list;watch;patch
+
+func newNodeFailureReconciler(client client.Client) *nodeFailureReconciler {
+	return &nodeFailureReconciler{
+		client: client,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName(TASNodeFailureController),
+		clock:  clock.RealClock{},
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager, cfg *config.Configuration) (string, error) {
+	return TASNodeFailureController, builder.ControllerManagedBy(mgr).
+		Named(TASNodeFailureController).
+		WatchesRawSource(source.TypedKind(
+			mgr.GetCache(),
+			&corev1.Node{},
+			&handler.TypedEnqueueRequestForObject[*corev1.Node]{},
+			r,
+		)).
+		For(&corev1.Node{}).
+		Complete(r)
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithValues("node", req.Name)
+	ctx = ctrl.LoggerInto(ctx, log)

+	var node corev1.Node
+	err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &node)
+	nodeExists := !apierrors.IsNotFound(err)
+	if err != nil && nodeExists {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to get Node")
+		return ctrl.Result{}, err
+	}
+
+	markFailed := false
+	var readyTransitionTime *metav1.Time
+	var readyStatus corev1.ConditionStatus
+	if nodeExists {
+		readyStatus, readyTransitionTime = r.getNodeConditionState(&node)
+		if readyStatus == corev1.ConditionTrue {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+		}

+			timeSinceNotReady := r.clock.Now().Sub(readyTransitionTime.Time)
+			if timeSinceNotReady >= NodeFailureDelay {
+				markFailed = true
+			} else {
+				return ctrl.Result{RequeueAfter: NodeFailureDelay - timeSinceNotReady}, nil
+			}
+		} else { // Node exists, not ready, but no transition time? Treat as failed immediately.
```

```diff
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithValues("node", req.Name)

+	var node corev1.Node
+	err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &node)
+	nodeExists := !apierrors.IsNotFound(err)
+	if err != nil && nodeExists {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to get Node")
+		return ctrl.Result{}, err
+	}

+	markFailed := false
+	var readyTransitionTime *metav1.Time
+	var readyStatus corev1.ConditionStatus
+	if nodeExists {
+		readyStatus, readyTransitionTime = r.getNodeConditionState(&node)
+		if readyStatus == corev1.ConditionTrue {

+		}
+		if readyTransitionTime != nil {

+				markFailed = true
+			} else {
+				return ctrl.Result{RequeueAfter: NodeFailureDelay - timeSinceNotReady}, nil
+			}
+		} else { // Node exists, not ready, but no transition time? Treat as failed immediately.
+			markFailed = true
+			log.V(2).Info("Node is not ready and NodeReady condition is missing or has an unexpected status, marking as failed immediately", "nodeName", node.Name)
+		}
+	} else {
+		log.V(3).Info("Node not found, assuming deleted")
+		markFailed = true
+	}
+
+	if markFailed {
+		if patchErr := r.patchWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx, req.Name); patchErr != nil {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, patchErr
+		}
+	}
+	return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+}
```

```diff
+// nodeFailureReconciler reconciles Nodes to detect failures and update affected Workloads
+type nodeFailureReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	clock  clock.Clock
+	log    logr.Logger
+}

+	return false
+}

+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Create(e event.TypedCreateEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	return true
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Update(e event.TypedUpdateEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	newNode := e.ObjectNew
+	if newNode == nil {
+		r.log.V(4).Info("Update event with nil object")
+		return false
+	}
+	if !utiltas.IsNodeStatusConditionTrue(newNode.Status.Conditions, corev1.NodeReady) {
+		r.log.V(4).Info("NodeReady is not true", "node", klog.KObj(newNode))
+		return true
+	}
+	r.log.V(5).Info("Node update does not warrant reconcile for failure detection", "node", klog.KObj(newNode))
+	return false
+}

+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Delete(e event.TypedDeleteEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	return true
+}

+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=nodes,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=pods,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads,verbs=get;list;watch;patch
+
+func newNodeFailureReconciler(client client.Client) *nodeFailureReconciler {
+	return &nodeFailureReconciler{
+		client: client,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName(TASNodeFailureController),
+		clock:  clock.RealClock{},
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager, cfg *config.Configuration) (string, error) {
+	return TASNodeFailureController, builder.ControllerManagedBy(mgr).
+		Named(TASNodeFailureController).
+		WatchesRawSource(source.TypedKind(
+			mgr.GetCache(),
+			&corev1.Node{},
+			&handler.TypedEnqueueRequestForObject[*corev1.Node]{},
+			r,
+		)).
+		For(&corev1.Node{}).
+		Complete(r)
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithValues("node", req.Name)
+	ctx = ctrl.LoggerInto(ctx, log)
+
+	log.V(3).Info("Getting node", "name", req.Name, "namespacename", req.NamespacedName)
+	var node corev1.Node
+	err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &node)
+	nodeExists := !apierrors.IsNotFound(err)
+	if err != nil && nodeExists {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to get Node")
+		return ctrl.Result{}, err
+	}
+
+	markFailed := false
+	var readyTransitionTime *metav1.Time
+	var readyStatus corev1.ConditionStatus
+	if nodeExists {
+		readyStatus, readyTransitionTime = r.getNodeConditionState(&node)
+		if readyStatus == corev1.ConditionTrue {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+		}
+		if readyTransitionTime != nil {
+			timeSinceNotReady := r.clock.Now().Sub(readyTransitionTime.Time)
+			if timeSinceNotReady >= NodeFailureDelay {
+				markFailed = true
+			} else {
+				return ctrl.Result{RequeueAfter: NodeFailureDelay - timeSinceNotReady}, nil
+			}
+		} else { // Node exists, not ready, but no transition time? Treat as failed immediately.
+			markFailed = true
+			log.V(2).Info("Node is not ready and NodeReady condition is missing or has an unexpected status, marking as failed immediately", "nodeName", node.Name)
+		}
+	} else {
+		log.V(3).Info("Node not found, assuming deleted")
+		markFailed = true
+	}
+
+	if markFailed {
+		if patchErr := r.patchWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx, req.Name); patchErr != nil {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, patchErr
+		}
+	}
+	return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+}
+
+// patchWorkloadsForNode finds workloads with pods on the specified node
+// and patches their status based on whether the node is currently considered failed.
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) patchWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx context.Context, nodeName string) error {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	var podList corev1.PodList
+	if err := r.client.List(ctx, &podList, client.MatchingFields{indexer.PodNodeNameIndexKey: nodeName}); err != nil {
+		log.V(2).Error(err, "Failed to list pods on node", "nodeName", nodeName)
+		return err
+	}
+	workloadsToProcess := sets.New[types.NamespacedName]()
+	for _, pod := range podList.Items {
+		if _, found := pod.GetLabels()[kueuealpha.TASLabel]; !found {
+			// skip non TAS pods
+			continue
+		}
+		if utilpod.IsTerminated(&pod) {
+			continue
+		}
+		wlName, found := pod.Annotations[kueuealpha.WorkloadAnnotation]
+		if !found {
+			continue
+		}
+		workloadsToProcess.Insert(types.NamespacedName{Name: wlName, Namespace: pod.Namespace})
+	}
+	var workloadProcessingErrors []error
+	for _, wlKey := range workloadsToProcess.UnsortedList() {
+		var wl kueue.Workload
+		if err := r.client.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wl); err != nil {
+			if apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
+				log.V(4).Info("Workload not found, skipping", "workload", wlKey)
+			} else {
+				log.V(2).Error(err, "Failed to get workload", "workload", wlKey)
+				workloadProcessingErrors = append(workloadProcessingErrors, err)
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		originalWl := wl.DeepCopy()
+		currentAnnotations := wl.GetAnnotations()
+		if currentAnnotations == nil {
+			currentAnnotations = make(map[string]string)
+		}
+		existingFailedNode, ok := currentAnnotations[kueuealpha.NodeToReplaceAnnotation]
+		if ok && existingFailedNode != "" && existingFailedNode != nodeName {
+			// TODO in this case we will start eviction of the workload due to multiple failed nodes
+			return nil
+		}
```

  Since this will be done in a separate PR, can we remove it from here for now

- **pkg/controller/tas/node_failure_controller.go:203** by [@PBundyra](https://github.com/PBundyra) — 2025-05-09T10:01:58Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,230 @@
+/*
+Copyright The Kubernetes Authors.
+
+Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+You may obtain a copy of the License at
+

+Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
+distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package tas
+
+import (
+	"context"
+	"errors"
+
+	"github.com/go-logr/logr"
+	corev1 "k8s.io/api/core/v1"
+	apierrors "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/api/errors"
+	metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/types"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/sets"
+	"k8s.io/klog/v2"
+	"k8s.io/utils/clock"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/builder"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/client"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/event"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/handler"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/predicate"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/reconcile"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime/pkg/source"
+
+	config "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/config/v1beta1"
+	kueuealpha "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1alpha1"
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/kueue/v1beta1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/controller/tas/indexer"
+	utilpod "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/util/pod"
+	utiltas "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/util/tas"
+)
+
+// nodeFailureReconciler reconciles Nodes to detect failures and update affected Workloads
+type nodeFailureReconciler struct {
+	client client.Client
+	clock  clock.Clock
+	log    logr.Logger
+}
+
+var _ reconcile.Reconciler = (*nodeFailureReconciler)(nil)
+var _ predicate.TypedPredicate[*corev1.Node] = (*nodeFailureReconciler)(nil)
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Generic(event.TypedGenericEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	return false
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Create(e event.TypedCreateEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	return true
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Update(e event.TypedUpdateEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	newNode := e.ObjectNew
+	if newNode == nil {
+		r.log.V(4).Info("Update event with nil object")
+		return false
+	}
+	if !utiltas.IsNodeStatusConditionTrue(newNode.Status.Conditions, corev1.NodeReady) {
+		r.log.V(4).Info("NodeReady is not true", "node", klog.KObj(newNode))
+		return true
+	}
+	r.log.V(5).Info("Node update does not warrant reconcile for failure detection", "node", klog.KObj(newNode))
+	return false
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Delete(e event.TypedDeleteEvent[*corev1.Node]) bool {
+	return true
+}
+
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=nodes,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups="",resources=pods,verbs=get;list;watch
+//+kubebuilder:rbac:groups=kueue.x-k8s.io,resources=workloads,verbs=get;list;watch;patch
+
+func newNodeFailureReconciler(client client.Client) *nodeFailureReconciler {
+	return &nodeFailureReconciler{
+		client: client,
+		log:    ctrl.Log.WithName(TASNodeFailureController),
+		clock:  clock.RealClock{},
+	}
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager, cfg *config.Configuration) (string, error) {
+	return TASNodeFailureController, builder.ControllerManagedBy(mgr).
+		Named(TASNodeFailureController).
+		WatchesRawSource(source.TypedKind(
+			mgr.GetCache(),
+			&corev1.Node{},
+			&handler.TypedEnqueueRequestForObject[*corev1.Node]{},
+			r,
+		)).
+		For(&corev1.Node{}).
+		Complete(r)
+}
+
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx).WithValues("node", req.Name)
+	ctx = ctrl.LoggerInto(ctx, log)
+
+	log.V(3).Info("Getting node", "name", req.Name, "namespacename", req.NamespacedName)
+	var node corev1.Node
+	err := r.client.Get(ctx, req.NamespacedName, &node)
+	nodeExists := !apierrors.IsNotFound(err)
+	if err != nil && nodeExists {
+		log.Error(err, "Failed to get Node")
+		return ctrl.Result{}, err
+	}
+
+	markFailed := false
+	var readyTransitionTime *metav1.Time
+	var readyStatus corev1.ConditionStatus
+	if nodeExists {
+		readyStatus, readyTransitionTime = r.getNodeConditionState(&node)
+		if readyStatus == corev1.ConditionTrue {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+		}
+		if readyTransitionTime != nil {
+			timeSinceNotReady := r.clock.Now().Sub(readyTransitionTime.Time)
+			if timeSinceNotReady >= NodeFailureDelay {
+				markFailed = true
+			} else {
+				return ctrl.Result{RequeueAfter: NodeFailureDelay - timeSinceNotReady}, nil
+			}
+		} else { // Node exists, not ready, but no transition time? Treat as failed immediately.
+			markFailed = true
+			log.V(2).Info("Node is not ready and NodeReady condition is missing or has an unexpected status, marking as failed immediately", "nodeName", node.Name)
+		}
+	} else {
+		log.V(3).Info("Node not found, assuming deleted")
+		markFailed = true
+	}
+
+	if markFailed {
+		if patchErr := r.patchWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx, req.Name); patchErr != nil {
+			return ctrl.Result{}, patchErr
+		}
+	}
+	return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+}
+
+// patchWorkloadsForNode finds workloads with pods on the specified node
+// and patches their status based on whether the node is currently considered failed.
+func (r *nodeFailureReconciler) patchWorkloadsForFailedNode(ctx context.Context, nodeName string) error {
+	log := ctrl.LoggerFrom(ctx)
+	var podList corev1.PodList
+	if err := r.client.List(ctx, &podList, client.MatchingFields{indexer.PodNodeNameIndexKey: nodeName}); err != nil {
+		log.V(2).Error(err, "Failed to list pods on node", "nodeName", nodeName)
+		return err
+	}
+	workloadsToProcess := sets.New[types.NamespacedName]()
+	for _, pod := range podList.Items {
+		if _, found := pod.GetLabels()[kueuealpha.TASLabel]; !found {
+			// skip non TAS pods
+			continue
+		}
+		if utilpod.IsTerminated(&pod) {
+			continue
+		}
+		wlName, found := pod.Annotations[kueuealpha.WorkloadAnnotation]
+		if !found {
+			continue
+		}
+		workloadsToProcess.Insert(types.NamespacedName{Name: wlName, Namespace: pod.Namespace})
+	}
+	var workloadProcessingErrors []error
+	for _, wlKey := range workloadsToProcess.UnsortedList() {
+		var wl kueue.Workload
+		if err := r.client.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wl); err != nil {
+			if apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
+				log.V(4).Info("Workload not found, skipping", "workload", wlKey)
+			} else {
+				log.V(2).Error(err, "Failed to get workload", "workload", wlKey)
+				workloadProcessingErrors = append(workloadProcessingErrors, err)
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		originalWl := wl.DeepCopy()
+		currentAnnotations := wl.GetAnnotations()
+		if currentAnnotations == nil {
+			currentAnnotations = make(map[string]string)
+		}
+		existingFailedNode, ok := currentAnnotations[kueuealpha.NodeToReplaceAnnotation]
+		if ok && existingFailedNode != "" && existingFailedNode != nodeName {
+			// TODO in this case we will start eviction of the workload due to multiple failed nodes
+			return nil
+		}
+		if ok && existingFailedNode == nodeName {
+			// nothing to do
+			return nil
```

  Do we want to exit the whole function instead of just continuing to another workload on the list?

```diff
+						break
+					}
+				}
+			})

+				setNodeCondition(ctx, k8sClient, node, corev1.NodeReady, corev1.ConditionFalse)
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("Waiting for controller to process node failure", func() {
+				time.Sleep(2 * time.Second)
+			})
```
